<user_id>116224749578238072054<//user_id><username>Team Irish<//username>< Time>
1521230610318</Time>
<Rating>5<//Rating><Review>UPDATE: STILL AWESOME
I still LOVE Oh My! Salon.  My original review of 5-stars still stands! A sign of a good place is also CONSISTENCY.  My most recent cut this weekend was just as great, if not better, than the first one because Allen actually still remembered me and how my hair was cut last time!  That was 6 months ago!

Allan has been cutting hair in the area for over 30 years.  You can't survive in this area for that long if you're not good.  I happen to be chatting with a neighbor and mentioned that I found a hairstylist that I really like.  When she found out who it was, she was so excited to find it was Allan because she used to go to him and LOVED him at his previous salon but wasn't sure what new location he was at. That says a lot about a hairstylist when customers are loyal.

******************************************
MY PREVIOUS REVIEW:

I HIGHLY RECOMMEND Oh My! and Allan, in particular, for haircuts!  I've lived all over the US, so I've had my hair cut from high-end salons in Manhattan, NY to suburban salons that have been around for decades in the West Coast so I've seen the whole spectrum.

FRIENDLY CUSTOMER SERVICE:
Julie who greeted me at the door was very warm and friendly.  Even though she was helping other customers, she acknowledged my entrance immediately.  Even Allan who was cutting a person's hair turned to smile at me.  It just shows their attentiveness and awareness of their customers.

CLEANLINESS:
Oh My is nice and clean...which is one of my top criteria when choosing a place.  Oh My keeps their floors swept/clean and the cutting stations are clean and uncluttered.

DETAILED-ORIENTED:
Allan listened to exactly what I was asking for. It was my first time at the salon, so he wanted to make sure he got to know my style and taste. I had asked to cut my hair 4 inches which was quite a bit for me, but he said he'd cut it 3-3.5 inches first to see if I liked the length and would cut it again if I wanted it shorter.  Even though it would mean more work for him, he wanted to make sure that I liked the length before he cut the 4 inches off the first time around because there would be no going back once it was cut. Of course, he was RIGHT! Once he cut it 3 inches, I realized I didn't want it any shorter. You can tell he's been cutting hair for a long time because he knew that I probably didn't want it as short as I thought.  What a save!

Allan was extremely detailed in his cutting...from checking the length in all directions to making corrections even after he dried my hair.

REASONABLE PRICING:
Again, as mentioned before, I've gotten trims in my life that were $125+ all the way to less than $20.  What I've learned is...more expensive DOES NOT mean better quality haircut. My shampooing, haircut, and blow dry came out to only $45 at Oh My! which is very reasonably priced considering the area and considering the quality service I received.

If your looking for a high quality haircut without having to pay for the "frills" that really don't matter (e.g., high-rent, fancy salon decor, etc.), then Oh My! is the place for you!  I would not hesitate to recommend this place to any of my friends.  I'll be going back again for sure!< /Review><Pics>None< /Pics><Response>None</Response><GmapID>0x808fbaf883a8a137:0xd236dafa9582fbe4< /GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<UserId.>107136176059594037309</UserId.><resp>None< /resp><username>Luis P.<//username><gmapID>0x80dc718f230fb069:0x7526f762d900045b<//gmapID><Time>1549470484980<//Time>< review>
The two stars are for the server, that despite the food fiasco, kept her desire to serve us well. No more excuses here for the so called cocineros dishing out the food. Plates ordered for a party of four that arrived hungry at around 7 PM:
Carnitas, $17.49. Average at best. Dry and the parts that were not were fat. Beans covered in salt. Rice slightly better. 3 Stars
Two Item Combo, Chicken Tamale and Chicken Flauta, $13.99. Tamale simply put: distasteful (where is a street vendor when you need a decent tamale?), the Flautas dry, bland, no love of cooking here. Beans salted with a vengeance. Rice easier to eat. 2 Stars.
Macho Combo, $16.99. Consisting of a fire-roasted padilla Chili Relleno, the best of the quartet. A Chicken and sour cream Quesadilla, a sad affair. A Beef Barbacoa crispy taco, with more lettuce than possible. Cheaply made, not appreciated, left almost intact. Hand made Chicken Tamale, who is kidding who here? Worst effort and absolute lack of redeeming qualities. Beans salted to no end, rice just okey. 1.5 Stars.
Baja Combo, $17.99. A slap to my the taste buds. Two bacon wrapped shrimp (by looking at the photo one believes they are going to be large and plump) these shrimp are a joke on the customer. Mahi- Mahi fish taco. Dry, barely any of it, a really sad and expensive fiasco. Mazatlan Enchilada: run, don't walk, avoid at all cost. Miniature Bay Shrimp, no more than two or three, with a sad excuse for a sauce. Beans horribly salted, rice no skills. 2 Stars.  Tortillas warm, salsa past its prime, one of the worst.
Cocineros (cooks) with either, or: resentment to management-low wages, no incentive to do better, no skills whatsoever, could not care any less.
Total: $71.61, plus a decent gratuity for the poor server who has to serve such badly made food. Money for nothing resembling quality. 2 Stars.<//review>

< Review>
It's nice that Korea-town has been popping up with more ramen joints around town. Often times you don't know if the place you're going to go to for Ramen is good, but Silverlake Ramen is a trusted brand and a household name. With their classic choices and new additions like the Garlic Truffle Ramen (5/5) which was rich and deep in flavor, combining the feeling of pasta with the luxury of ramen. Service here is really nice too, the guys are awesome and they strike up a friendly conversation with you.

Lastly, even though I'm writing this review during covid season, I must say, the seating area here in the plaza is very nice. Private in a way, and it feels like a mini farmers market, the ambiance is very nice, and for that, it got bumped up from 4 stars to 5 stars.

Enjoy dining in!</Review>
